What is an </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>? Bibles are translated into each of our languages from the original Hebrew, Aramaic, and Koine Greek. Occasionally, the best word translation cannot be found and these words are transliterated letter by letter. Four well known transliterations are </Value><I><Value>Christ</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>baptism</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>angel</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>apostle</Value></I><Value>. The meaning is then preserved more accurately through context and a dictionary. The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates eleven additional Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The first three words are </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, typically translated as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> and also </Value><I><Value>world</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value>. The Aionian Bible is named after an alternative spelling of </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value>. Consider that researchers question if </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> actually mean </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value>. Translating </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> in Matthew 28:20 makes no sense, as all agree. The Greek word for </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> is </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, used in Romans 1:20 about God and in Jude 6 about demon imprisonment. Yet what about </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> in John 3:16? Certainly we do not question whether salvation is eternal! However, </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> means something much more wonderful than infinite time! Ancient Greeks used </Value><I><Value>aiōn</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value>. They also used the adjective </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>entirety</Value></I><Value>, such as </Value><I><Value>complete</Value></I><Value> or even </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value>, but never infinite time. Read Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan for proofs. So </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> is the perfect description of God's Word which has </Value><I><Value>everything</Value></I><Value> we need for life and godliness! And the </Value><I><Value>aiōnios</Value></I><Value> life promised in John 3:16 is not simply a ticket to eternal life in the future, but the invitation through faith to the </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> life beginning now!</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The next seven words are </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value>. These words are often translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>, the place of eternal punishment. However, </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is ill-defined when compared with the Hebrew and Greek. For example, </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> is the abode of deceased believers and unbelievers and should never be translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value> is a temporary place of punishment, Revelation 20:13-14. </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value> is the Valley of Hinnom, Jerusalem's refuse dump, a temporal judgment for sin. </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value> is a prison for demons, mentioned once in 2 Peter 2:4. </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value> is a temporary prison for the Beast and Satan. Translators are also inconsistent because </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is used by the King James Version 54 times, the New International Version 14 times, and the World English Bible zero times. Finally, </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value> is the Lake of Fire, yet Matthew 25:41 explains that these fires are prepared for the Devil and his angels. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The eleventh word,  </Value><I><Value>eleēsē</Value></I><Value>, reveals the grand conclusion of grace in Romans 11:32. Take the time to understand these eleven words. The original translation is unaltered and a note is added to 64 Old Testament and 201 New Testament verses. To help parallel study and Strong's Concordance use, apocryphal text is removed and most variant verse numbering is mapped to the English standard. The original translation is unaltered and notes are added to help your study. The notes show the location of eleven special Greek and Hebrew Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and for all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Who has the authority to interpret the Bible and examine the underlying Hebrew and Greek words? That is a good question! We read in 1 John 2:27, </Value><I><Value>“As for you, the anointing which you received from him remains in you, and you do not need for anyone to teach you. But as his anointing teaches you concerning all things, and is true, and is no lie, and even as it taught you, you remain in him.”</Value></I><Value> Every Christian is qualified to interpret the Bible! Now that does not mean we will all agree. Each of us is still growing in our understanding of the truth. However, it does mean that there is no infallible human or tradition to answer all our questions. Instead the Holy Spirit helps each of us to know the truth and grow closer to God and each other.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Bible is a library with 66 books in the Protestant Canon. The best way to learn God’s word is to read entire books. Read the book of Genesis. Read the book of John. Read the entire Bible library. Topical studies and cross-referencing can be good. However, the safest way to understand context and meaning is to read whole Bible books. Chapter and verse numbers were added for convenience in the 16th century, but unfortunately they can cause the Bible to seem like an encyclopedia. The Aionian Bible is formatted with simple verse numbering, minimal notes, and no cross-referencing in order to encourage the reading of Bible books.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Bible reading must also begin with prayer. Any Christian is qualified to interpret the Bible with God’s help. However, this freedom is also a responsibility because without the Holy Spirit we cannot interpret accurately. We read in 1 Corinthians 2:13-14, </Value><I><Value>“And we speak of these things, not with words taught by human wisdom, but with those taught by the Spirit, comparing spiritual things with spiritual things. Now the natural person does not receive the things of the Spirit of God, for they are foolishness to him, and he cannot understand them, because they are spiritually discerned.”</Value></I><Value> So we cannot understand in our natural self, but we can with God’s help through prayer.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Holy Spirit is the best writer and he uses literary devices such as introductions, conclusions, paragraphs, and metaphors. He also writes various genres including historical narrative, prose, and poetry. So Bible study must spiritually discern and understand literature. Pray, read, observe, interpret, and apply. Finally, </Value><I><Value>“Do your best to present yourself approved by God, a worker who does not need to be ashamed, properly handling the word of truth.”</Value></I><Value> 2 Timothy 2:15. </Value><I><Value>“God has granted to us his precious and exceedingly great promises; that through these you may become partakers of the divine nature, having escaped from the corruption that is in the world by lust. Yes, and for this very cause adding on your part all diligence, in your faith supply moral excellence; and in moral excellence, knowledge; and in knowledge, self-control; and in self-control patience; and in patience godliness; and in godliness brotherly affection; and in brotherly affection, love. For if these things are yours and abound, they make you to be not idle nor unfruitful to the knowledge of our Lord Jesus Christ,”</Value></I><Value> 2 Peter 1:4-8.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Glossary</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Glossar</Value></U><Value>y</Value></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates eleven special words to help us better understand the extent of God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies. Compare the meanings below to the Strong's Concordance and Glossary definitions.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Glos'><Value>Abyssos </Value></Fontface></I></B><Value> g12</Value><Br /><I><Value>Greek:</Value></I><Value> proper noun, place</Value><Br /><I><Value>Usage:</Value></I><Value> 9 times in 3 books, 6 chapters, and 9 verses</Value><Br /><I><Value>Meaning:</Value></I><Br /><HSpace width='0.25in'/><Value>Temporary prison for special fallen angels such as Apollyon, the Beast, and Satan.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Glos'><Value>aïdios </Value></Fontface></I></B><Value> g126</Value><Br /><I><Value>Greek:</Value></I><Value> adjective</Value><Br /><I><Value>Usage:</Value></I><Value> 2 times in Romans 1:20 and Jude 6</Value><Br /><I><Value>Meaning:</Value></I><Br /><HSpace width='0.25in'/><Value>Lasting, enduring forever, eternal.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Glos'><Value>aiōn </Value></Fontface></I></B><Value> g165</Value><Br /><I><Value>Greek:</Value></I><Value> noun</Value><Br /><I><Value>Usage:</Value></I><Value> 127 times in 22 books, 75 chapters, and 102 verses</Value><Br /><I><Value>Meaning:</Value></I><Br /><HSpace width='0.25in'/><Value>A lifetime or time period with a beginning and end, an era, an age, the completion of which is beyond human perception, but known only to God the creator of the aiōns, Hebrews 1:2. Never meaning simple endless or infinite chronological time in Greek usage. Read Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan for proofs.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Glos'><Value>aiōnios </Value></Fontface></I></B><Value> g166</Value><Br /><I><Value>Greek:</Value></I><Value> adjective</Value><Br /><I><Value>Usage:</Value></I><Value> 71 times in 19 books, 44 chapters, and 69 verses</Value><Br /><I><Value>Meaning:</Value></I><Br /><HSpace width='0.25in'/><Value>From start to finish, pertaining to the age, lifetime, entirety, complete, or even consummate. Never meaning simple endless or infinite chronological time in Koine Greek usage. Read Dr. Heleen Keizer and Ramelli and Konstan for proofs.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Glos'><Value>eleēsē </Value></Fontface></I></B><Value> g1653</Value><Br /><I><Value>Greek:</Value></I><Value> verb, aorist tense, active voice, subjunctive mood, 3rd person singular</Value><Br /><I><Value>Usage:</Value></I><Value> 1 time in this conjugation, Romans 11:32</Value><Br /><I><Value>Meaning:</Value></I><Br /><HSpace width='0.25in'/><Value>To have pity on, to show mercy. Typically, the subjunctive mood indicates possiblity, not certainty. However, a subjunctive in a purpose clause is a resulting action as certain as the causal action. The subjunctive in a purpose clause functions as an indicative, not an optative. Thus, the grand conclusion of grace theology in Romans 11:32 must be clarified. God's mercy on all is not a possibility, but a certainty. See </Value><U><Value>nt</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>reek.or</Value></U><Value>g.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><B><I><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Bibles/English---Aionian-Bible/Noted</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Glossary references are below. Strong's Hebrew and Greek number notes are added to 64 Old Testament and 201 New Testament verses. Questioned verse translations do not contain Aionian Glossary words and may wrongly imply </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. * The note placement is skipped or adjusted for verses with non-standard numbering.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Destiny</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Destiny</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible shows the location of eleven special Greek and Hebrew Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and for all mankind, and the nature of after-life destinies. The underlying Hebrew and Greek words typically translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> show us that there are not just two after-life destinies, Heaven or Hell. Instead, there are a number of different locations, each with different purposes, different durations, and different inhabitants. Locations include 1) Old Testament </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> and New Testament </Value><I><Value>Hadēs</Value></I><Value>, 2) </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, 3) </Value><I><Value>Tartaroō</Value></I><Value>, 4) </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, 5) </Value><I><Value>Limnē Pyr</Value></I><Value>, 6) </Value><I><Value>Paradise</Value></I><Value>, 7) </Value><I><Value>The New Heaven</Value></I><Value>, and 8) </Value><I><Value>The New Earth</Value></I><Value>. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The key observation is that fallen angels will be present at the final judgment, 2 Peter 2:4 and Jude 6. Traditionally, we understand the separation of the Sheep and the Goats at the final judgment to divide believing from unbelieving mankind, Matthew 25:31-46 and Revelation 20:11-15. However, the presence of fallen angels alternatively suggests that Jesus is separating redeemed mankind from the fallen angels. We do know that Jesus is the helper of mankind and not the helper of the Devil, Hebrews 2. We also know that Jesus has atoned for the sins of all mankind, both believer and unbeliever alike, 1 John 2:1-2. Deceased believers are rewarded in Paradise, Luke 23:43, while unbelievers are punished in Hades as the story of Lazarus makes plain, Luke 16:19-31. Yet less commonly known, the punishment of this selfish man and all unbelievers is before the final judgment, is temporal, and is punctuated when Hades is evacuated, Revelation 20:13. So is there hope beyond Hades for unbelieving mankind? Jesus promised, </Value><I><Value>“the gates of Hades will not prevail,”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 16:18. Paul asks, </Value><I><Value>“Hades where is your victory?”</Value></I><Value> 1 Corinthians 15:55. John wrote, </Value><I><Value>“Hades gives up,”</Value></I><Value> Revelation 20:13.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Jesus comforts us saying, </Value><I><Value>“Do not be afraid,”</Value></I><Value> because he holds the keys to </Value><I><Value>unlock</Value></I><Value> death and Hades, Revelation 1:18. Yet too often our </Value><I><Value>Good News</Value></I><Value> sounds like a warning to </Value><I><Value>“be afraid”</Value></I><Value> because Jesus holds the keys to </Value><I><Value>lock</Value></I><Value> Hades! Wow, we have it backwards! Hades will be evacuated! And to guarrantee hope, once emptied, Hades is thrown into the Lake of Fire, never needed again, Revelation 20:14.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Finally, we read that anyone whose name is not written in the Book of Life is thrown into the Lake of Fire, the second death, with no exit ever mentioned or promised, Revelation 21:1-8. So are those evacuated from Hades then, </Value><I><Value>“out of the frying pan, into the fire?”</Value></I><Value> Certainly, the Lake of Fire is the destiny of the Goats. But, do not be afraid. Instead, read the Bible's explicit mention of the purpose of the Lake of Fire and the identity of the Goats, </Value><I><Value>“Then he will say also to those on the left hand, ‘Depart from me, you cursed, into the consummate fire which is prepared for... the devil and his angels,’”</Value></I><Value> Matthew 25:41. Bad news for the Devil. Good news for all mankind!</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Faith is not a pen to write your own name in the Book of Life. Instead, faith is the glasses to see that the love of Christ for all mankind has already written our names in Heaven. Jesus said, </Value><I><Value>“You did not choose me, but I chose you,” John 15:16</Value></I><Value>. Though unbelievers will suffer regrettable punishment in Hades, redeemed mankind will never enter the Lake of Fire, prepared for the devil and his angels. And as God promised, all mankind will worship Christ together forever, Philippians 2:9-11.</Value></Paragraph>	GOOD		Preface				APPENDIX	Reader's Guide	Glossary	Maps	Illustrations	Destiny																											END

Luka 23:34	Dhe unë, Gjoni, pashë qytetin e shenjtë, Jeruzalemin e ri, që zbriste nga qielli, nga Perëndia, që ishte bërë gati si nuse e stolisur për burrin e vet. Dhe dëgjova një zë të madh nga qielli që thoshte: “Ja tabernakulli i Perëndisë me njerëzit! Dhe ai do të banojë me ta; edhe ata do të jenë populli i tij dhe vetë Perëndia do të jetë bashkë me ta, Perëndi e tyre.	Zbulesa 21:2-3	Me anë të besimit Abrahami, kur u thirr, u bind të shkojë në atë vend që do të merrte për trashëgim; dhe u nis pa ditur se ku po shkonte.</Value><Br /><Value>	Hebrenjve 11:8	Kur Faraoni e la popullin të shkojë, Perëndia nuk e çoi nëpër rrugën e vendit të Filistejve, megjithëse kjo ishte më e shkurtëra, sepse Perëndia tha:</Value><Br /><Value>“Që të mos pendohet populli, kur të shohë luftën, dhe të mos kthehet në Egjipt”.	Eksodi 13:17	Sepse edhe Biri i njeriut nuk erdhi që t’i shërbejnë, por për të shërbyer dhe për të dhënë jetën e tij si çmim për shpengimin e shumë vetave.	Marku 10:45	Pali, shërbëtor i Jezu Krishtit, i thirrur për të qenë apostull, i veçuar për ungjillin e Perëndisë,	Romakëve 1:1	Shkoni, pra, dhe bëni dishepuj nga të gjithë popujt duke i pagëzuar në emër të Atit e të Birit e të Frymës së Shenjtë,	Mateu 28:19	END

المحتويات	الملحق	دليل القارئ	المعجم	خرائط	الرسوم التوضيحية	مصير	حياة	ترجمة الكتاب المقدس الأول في العالم عكس	100% مجانا لنسخ وطباعة	المعروف أيضا باسم	الكتاب المقدس الأرجواني	FOREIGN		6	لِأَنَّهُ هَكَذَا أَحَبَّ ٱللهُ ٱلْعَالَمَ حَتَّى بَذَلَ ٱبْنَهُ ٱلْوَحِيدَ، لِكَيْ لَا يَهْلِكَ كُلُّ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ، بَلْ تَكُونُ لَهُ ٱلْحَيَاةُ ٱلْأَبَدِيَّةُ.	يوحنَّا ٣:١٦	فَطَرَدَ ٱلْإِنْسَانَ، وَأَقَامَ شَرْقِيَّ جَنَّةِ عَدْنٍ ٱلْكَرُوبِيمَ، وَلَهِيبَ سَيْفٍ مُتَقَلِّبٍ لِحِرَاسَةِ طَرِيقِ شَجَرَةِ ٱلْحَيَاةِ.	اَلتَّكْوِينُ ٣:٢٤	فَقَالَ يَسُوعُ: «يَا أَبَتَاهُ، ٱغْفِرْ لَهُمْ، لِأَنَّهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ مَاذَا يَفْعَلُونَ». وَإِذِ ٱقْتَسَمُوا ثِيَابَهُ ٱقْتَرَعُوا عَلَيْهَا.	لُوقا ٢٣:٣٤	وَأَنَا يُوحَنَّا رَأَيْتُ ٱلْمَدِينَةَ ٱلْمُقَدَّسَةَ أُورُشَلِيمَ ٱلْجَدِيدَةَ نَازِلَةً مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاءِ مِنْ عِنْدِ ٱللهِ مُهَيَّأَةً كَعَرُوسٍ مُزَيَّنَةٍ لِرَجُلِهَا. وَسَمِعْتُ صَوْتًا عَظِيمًا مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاءِ قَائِلًا: «هُوَذَا مَسْكَنُ ٱللهِ مَعَ ٱلنَّاسِ، وَهُوَ سَيَسْكُنُ مَعَهُمْ، وَهُمْ يَكُونُونَ لَهُ شَعْبًا، وَٱللهُ نَفْسُهُ يَكُونُ مَعَهُمْ إِلَهًا لَهُمْ.	رُؤيا ٢١:٢-٣	بِٱلْإِيمَانِ إِبْرَاهِيمُ لَمَّا دُعِيَ أَطَاعَ أَنْ يَخْرُجَ إِلَى ٱلْمَكَانِ ٱلَّذِي كَانَ عَتِيدًا أَنْ يَأْخُذَهُ مِيرَاثًا، فَخَرَجَ وَهُوَ لَا يَعْلَمُ إِلَى أَيْنَ يَأْتِي.	عِبرانِيّين ١١:٨	وَكَانَ لَمَّا أَطْلَقَ فِرْعَوْنُ ٱلشَّعْبَ أَنَّ ٱللهَ لَمْ يَهْدِهِمْ فِي طَرِيقِ أَرْضِ ٱلْفِلِسْطِينِيِّينَ مَعَ أَنَّهَا قَرِيبَةٌ، لِأَنَّ ٱللهَ قَالَ: «لِئَلَّا يَنْدَمَ ٱلشَّعْبُ إِذَا رَأَوْا حَرْبًا وَيَرْجِعُوا إِلَى مِصْرَ».	اَلْخُرُوجُ ١٣:١٧	لِأَنَّ ٱبْنَ ٱلْإِنْسَانِ أَيْضًا لَمْ يَأْتِ لِيُخْدَمَ بَلْ لِيَخْدِمَ وَلِيَبْذِلَ نَفْسَهُ فِدْيَةً عَنْ كَثِيرِينَ».	مَرْقُس ١٠:٤٥	بُولُسُ، عَبْدٌ لِيَسُوعَ ٱلْمَسِيحِ، ٱلْمَدْعُوُّ رَسُولًا، ٱلْمُفْرَزُ لِإِنْجِيلِ ٱللهِ،	رُوما ١:١	فَٱذْهَبُوا وَتَلْمِذُوا جَمِيعَ ٱلْأُمَمِ وَعَمِّدُوهُمْ بِٱسْمِ ٱلْآبِ وَٱلِٱبْنِ وَٱلرُّوحِ ٱلْقُدُسِ.	مَتَّى ٢٨:١٩	END

أَحَبَّ اللهُ الْعَالَمَ حَتَّى بَذَلَ ابْنَهُ الْوَحِيدَ، لِكَيْ لاَ يَهْلِكَ كُلُّ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِهِ، بَلْ تَكُونُ لَهُ الْحَيَاةُ الأَبَدِيَّةُ.	يوحنَّا ٣:١٦	وَهَكَذَا طَرَدَ اللهُ الإِنْسَانَ مِنْ جَنَّةِ عَدْنٍ، وَأَقَامَ مَلائِكَةَ الْكَرُوبِيمِ وَسَيْفاً نَارِيّاً مُتَقَلِّباً شَرْقِيَّ الْجَنَّةِ لِحِرَاسَةِ الطَّرِيقِ الْمُفْضِيَةِ إِلَى «شَجَرَةِ الْحَيَاةِ».	تكوين ٣:٢٤	وَقَالَ يَسُوعُ: «يَاأَبِي، اغْفِرْ لَهُمْ، لأَنَّهُمْ لاَ يَدْرُونَ مَا يَفْعَلُونَ!» وَاقْتَسَمُوا ثِيَابَهُ مُقْتَرِعِينَ عَلَيْهَا.	لُوقا ٢٣:٣٤	وَأَنَا رَأَيْتُ الْمَدِينَةَ الْمُقَدَّسَةَ، أُورُشَلِيمَ الْجَدِيدَةَ، نَازِلَةً مِنَ السَّمَاءِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللهِ، مُجَهَّزَةً كَأَنَّهَا عَرُوسٌ مُزَيَّنَةٌ لِعَرِيسِهَا. وَسَمِعْتُ صَوْتاً هَاتِفاً مِنَ الْعَرْشِ: «الآنَ صَارَ مَسْكِنُ اللهِ مَعَ النَّاسِ، هُوَ يَسْكُنُ بَيْنَهُمْ، وَهُمْ يَصِيرُونَ شَعْباً لَهُ. اللهُ نَفْسُهُ يَكُونُ مَعَهُمْ إِلهاً لَهُمْ!	رُؤيا ٢١:٢-٣	وَبِالإِيمَانِ، لَبَّى إِبْرَاهِيمُ دَعْوَةَ اللهِ، فَتَرَكَ وَطَنَهُ وَانْطَلَقَ إِلَى أَرْضٍ أُخْرَى وَعَدَهُ اللهُ بِأَنْ يُوَرِّثَهُ إِيَّاهَا. وَلَمَّا خَرَجَ مِنْ بَيْتِهِ، لَمْ يَكُنْ يَعْرِفُ أَيْنَ يَتَوَجَّهُ.	عِبرانِيّين ١١:٨	وَعِنْدَمَا أَطْلَقَ فِرْعَوْنُ الشَّعْبَ لَمْ يَقُدْهُمُ اللهُ فِي طَرِيقِ بِلاَدِ الْفِلِسْطِينِيِّينَ عَلَى الرَّغْمِ مِنْ قِصَرِهَا. لأَنَّ اللهَ قَالَ لِئَلاَّ يَنْدَمَ الشَّعْبُ إِذَا تَعَرَّضَ لِحَرْبٍ وَيَرْجِعَ إِلَى مِصْرَ.	خرُوج ١٣:١٧	فَحَتَّى ابْنُ الإِنْسَانِ قَدْ جَاءَ لاَ لِيُخْدَمَ، بَلْ لِيَخْدِمَ وَيَبْذِلَ نَفْسَهُ فِدْيَةً عَنْ كَثِيرِينَ».	مَرْقُس ١٠:٤٥	مِنْ بُولُسَ عَبْدِ يَسُوعَ المَسِيحِ، الرَّسُولِ الْمَدْعُوِّ وَالْمُفْرَزِ لإِنْجِيلِ اللهِ،	رُوما ١:١	فَاذْهَبُوا إِذَنْ، وَتَلْمِذُوا جَمِيعَ الأُمَمِ، وَعَمِّدُوهُمْ بِاسْمِ الآبِ وَالاِبْنِ وَالرُّوحِ الْقُدُسِ؛	مَتَّى ٢٨:١٩	END

আর বরের জন্য সাজানো কন্যের মত এই শহরকে সাজানো হয়েছিল। পরে আমি সিংহাসন থেকে একটা জোরে কন্ঠস্বর শুনতে পেলাম, দেখ, মানুষের সঙ্গে ঈশ্বরের এখন থাকার বাসস্থান হয়েছে এবং তিনি তাদের সঙ্গে বাস করবেন। তারা তাঁর প্রজা হবে এবং ঈশ্বর নিজে মানুষের সঙ্গে থাকবেন এবং তিনি তাদের ঈশ্বর হবেন।	প্রকাশিত বাক্য ২১:২-৩	বিশ্বাসে অব্রাহাম, যখন তিনি মনোনীত হলেন, তিনি ঈশ্বরের বাধ্য হলেন এবং তিনি যে জায়গা পাবেন তা অধিকার করতে চলে গেলেন। তিনি কোথায় যাচ্ছেন, তা না জেনে রওনা দিলেন।	ইব্রীয় ১১:৮	আর ফরৌণ লোকদের ছেড়ে দিলে, পলেষ্টীয়দের দেশ দিয়ে সোজা পথ থাকলেও ঈশ্বর সেই পথে তাদেরকে যেতে দিলেন না, কারণ ঈশ্বর বললেন, “যুদ্ধ দেখলে হয়তো লোকেরা অনুতাপ করে মিশরে ফিরে যাবে।”	যাত্রাপুস্তক ১৩:১৭	কারণ মনুষ্যপুত্র জগতে সেবা পেতে আসেনি, কিন্তু অপরের সেবা করতে এসেছে এবং মানুষের জন্য নিজের জীবন মুক্তির মূল্য হিসাবে দিতে এসেছেন।	মার্ক ১০:৪৫	পৌল, একজন যীশু খ্রীষ্টের দাস, প্রেরিত হবার জন্য ডাকা হয়েছে এবং ঈশ্বরের সুসমাচার প্রচারের জন্য আলাদা ভাবে মনোনীত করেছেন,	রোমীয় ১:১	অতএব তোমরা গিয়ে সমস্ত জাতিকে শিষ্য কর, পিতার ও পুত্রের ও পবিত্র আত্মার নামে তাদের বাপ্তিষ্ম দাও,	মথি ২৮:১৯	END

Holy-Bible---English---Aionian-Bible				TRUE	TRUE	978-0-35939-420-3	978-1-67811-695-8	978-1-67811-689-7	978-0-35937-112-9	04e29fcb-7128-60f9-f983-d6c06665c923			Aionian Bible	Aionian Bible																		FF-Copy	FF-VerE	758												<Paragraph textformat='center' fontfamily='FF-Head'><Value>Preface</Value><Br /><Fontface fontfamily='FF-Pref'><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Preface</Value></U></Fontface></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The </Value><I><Value>Holy Bible Aionian Edition ®</Value></I><Value> is the world’s first Bible </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>! What is an </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value>? Bibles are translated into each of our languages from the original Hebrew, Aramaic, and Greek. Occasionally, the best word translation cannot be found and these words are transliterated letter by letter. Four well known transliterations are </Value><I><Value>Christ</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>baptism</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>angel</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>apostle</Value></I><Value>. The meaning is then preserved more accurately through context and a dictionary. The Aionian Bible un-translates and instead transliterates eleven additional Aionian Glossary words to help us better understand God’s love for individuals and all mankind, and the nature of afterlife destinies.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The Aionian Bible </Value><I><Value>un-translation</Value></I><Value> helps us to see these eleven underlying words in context. Actually, the original translation is unaltered and a note is added to 64 Old Testament and 201 New Testament verses. Also the Aionian Bible is not one Bible, but an entire library of public domain and Creative Common Bible texts. In each of the Bible republications the original text is wholly unaltered, except for this particular translation which is specifically named the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. The </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation is a new translation identical to the public domain </Value><I><Value>World English Bible Updated</Value></I><Value> except for the retranslation of the verses containing Aionian Glossary words and a few additional verses are revised to correspond with the underlying Hebrew and Greek. This new translation includes the same inline notes as every Bible in the Aionian Bible library, but also retranslates the Aionian Glossary words to more accurately reflect the underlying Hebrew and Greek words. Every verse retranslation in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation is based on meticulous reference to the underlying language sources. The </Value><I><Value>World English Bible Updated</Value></I><Value> was chosen as a base text simply because it is the most readable public domain English translation.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The first three Greek words reconsidered are </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, typically translated as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> and also </Value><I><Value>world</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value>. In fact, the Aionian Bible is named after an alternative spelling of </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>. Consider that researchers question if </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> actually mean </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value>. Translating </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> as </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> in Matthew 28:20 makes no sense, as all agree. The Greek word for </Value><I><Value>eternal</Value></I><Value> is </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value>, used in Romans 1:20 about God and in Jude 6 about demon imprisonment. Therefore, </Value><I><Value>aïdios</Value></I><Value> remains translated as </Value><I><Value>everlasting</Value></I><Value> in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. Yet what about </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> in John 3:16? Certainly we do not question whether salvation is eternal! However, </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> means something much more wonderful than infinite time! Ancient Greeks used </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> or </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value>. The similar spelling of </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>eon</Value></I><Value> is easily seen. They also used the adjective </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> to mean </Value><I><Value>entirety</Value></I><Value>, such as </Value><I><Value>complete</Value></I><Value> or even </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value>, but never infinite time. Thus </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> is retranslated </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> 65 times, </Value><I><Value>of the ages</Value></I><Value> two times, and </Value><I><Value>wholly</Value></I><Value> one time in the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value> translation. </Value><I><Value>Aion</Value></I><Value> is retranslated as </Value><I><Value>age</Value></I><Value> 95 times and </Value><I><Value>lifetime</Value></I><Value> two times. Note that familiar Hebrews verses now say more accurately, and perhaps even more poetically, '</Value><I><Value>Jesus is a priest for the age.</Value></I><Value>'</Value></Paragraph> <Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The wonderful rediscovery is that the </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value> life promised in John 3:16 is not simply a ticket to eternal life in the future, but the invitation through faith to the </Value><I><Value>consummate</Value></I><Value> life beginning now! </Value><I><Value>Aionios</Value></I><Value> is the perfect description of God's Word which has </Value><I><Value>everything</Value></I><Value> we need for life and godliness.</Value></Paragraph>	<Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The next seven words are </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Hades</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Tartaroo</Value></I><Value>, </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value>, and </Value><I><Value>Limne Pyr</Value></I><Value>. These words are often translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>, the place of eternal punishment. However, </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is ill-defined when compared with the Hebrew and Greek. For example, </Value><I><Value>Sheol</Value></I><Value> is the abode of deceased believers and unbelievers and should never be translated as </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value>. </Value><I><Value>Hades</Value></I><Value> is a temporary place of punishment, Revelation 20:13-14. </Value><I><Value>Geenna</Value></I><Value> is the Valley of Hinnom, Jerusalem's refuse dump, a temporal judgment for sin. </Value><I><Value>Tartaroo</Value></I><Value> is a prison for demons, mentioned once in 2 Peter 2:4. </Value><I><Value>Abyssos</Value></I><Value> is a temporary prison for the Beast and Satan. Translators are also inconsistent because </Value><I><Value>Hell</Value></I><Value> is used by the King James Version 54 times, the New International Version 14 times, and the </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> zero times. Finally, </Value><I><Value>Limne Pyr</Value></I><Value> is the Lake of Fire, yet Matthew 25:41 explains that these fires are prepared for the Devil and his angels. So there is reason to review our conclusions about the destinies of redeemed mankind and fallen angels.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>The eleventh word, </Value><I><Value>eleēsē</Value></I><Value>, reveals the grand conclusion of grace in Romans 11:32. Take the time to understand these eleven words. The Aionian Bible project invites you to reconsider traditional Christian understanding. It may seem utterly ridiculous to suggest that the most well-known verse in the history of Christianity, John 3:16, was improperly translated. And it may seem preposterous to propose that a destiny of Heaven or Hell is not the complete picture. Yet is it ridiculous? Is it preposterous? Have we or our forefathers ever carried ignorance and errors along for decades and even centuries in the past? We have. Even so, the purpose of the Aionian Bible project is not to abandon tradition or Christian heritage. We have much to learn from the belief and practice of godly men and women throughout all ages. Instead the purpose of this project is to invite us to compare our current conclusions with Scripture. We should never be afraid to review our understanding. Do consider Dr. Heleen Keizer's article </Value><I><Value>'ETERNITY REVISITED' A Study of the Greek Word aion</Value></I><Value> and other resources at </Value><U><Value>AionianBible.or</Value></U><Value>g</Value><U><Value>/Aionios-and-Aidios</Value></U><Value>. This article is a useful introduction to the first century usage and meaning of </Value><I><Value>aion</Value></I><Value> and </Value><I><Value>aionios</Value></I><Value>. Further resources can be found countless places online and in print. Then study the Scripture and ask the Lord for understanding. Hopefully you find this invitation to reconsider fair, thought-provoking, and above all, honoring to God's Word.</Value></Paragraph><Paragraph textformat='prefaceparagraph' fontfamily='FF-Pref'><Value>Again, the original text for each translation in the Aionian Bible library is unaltered, except for this particular Bible named the </Value><I><Value>Aionian Bible</Value></I><Value>, which is itself a new translation based on the </Value><I><Value>World English Bible</Value></I><Value> as explained above. Holy-Bible---English---STEPBible-Amalgamant				TRUE	TRUE	UNKNOWN		UNKNOWN	UNKNOWN	e9e7664a-999e-3866-f0b0-09aceb940864			STEPBible, Amalgamant	STEPBible, Amalgamant																		FF-Copy	FF-VerE	800		8.2000	10.3000	125.61%		2.1000				This text is a Bible translator resource from the STEPBible Tyndale Amalgamated Hebrew and Greek. The Old and New Testament tag legend is found online at https://www.aionianbible.org/Bibles/English---STEPBible-Amalgamant. New Testament study is revolutionized by the discovery of earlier manuscripts in the North African sands and other discoveries.  The NA text is based mostly on these earlier manuscripts, but the TR text was compiled from later ones, before the earlier ones were found. Later scribes often removed ambiguities with changes like adding the name 'Jesus' instead of 'he', adding prepositions such as 'with' and 'to' instead of relying on Greek dative and genitive cases, and occasionally adding phrases to clarify the text. There are no instances of changed theology, confirmed by the huge failed effort to find even one. Less discussed are the words found in the earlier manuscripts, but not in the later.  Of these, there are 548 differences with no impact to meaning, and 277 scribal clarification differences. And these are only mildly significant changes like '72' for '70' disciples sent out in Luke 10:1,17, 'Spirit of Jesus' for 'Jesus' in Acts 16:7, 'as you now walk' in 1Th 4:1, 'according to God' in 1Pet 5:2, 'show mercy to others' in Jude 23, and 'and a third of the earth was burned' in Rev 8:7. The best explanation is that additions found only in earlier manuscripts and additions found only in later ones are simply two sets of additions by scribes to clarify the text with no theological agenda. So, if you want the very earliest text, use only the words that are in both NA and TR. If you want to include clarifications by North African believers like modern Bibles, then include words found only in NA. If you want to only include the clarifications by Byzantine scribes like the KJV, then include the words found only in TR, and use the TR variants.	<Paragraph textformat='leftpad' fontfamily='FF-Copy'><Value>This text is a Bible translator resource from the STEPBible Tyndale Amalgamated Hebrew and Greek. નથી.’</Value><Br /><Value>ચિઠ્ઠીઓ નાખીને તેઓએ તેમના વસ્ત્ર અંદરોઅંદર વહેંચી લીધા.	લૂક ૨૩:૩૪	મેં પવિત્ર નગર, નવું યરુશાલેમ, ઈશ્વરની પાસેથી સ્વર્ગમાંથી ઊતરતું જોયું, અને જેમ કન્યા પોતાના વરને સારુ શણગારેલી હોય તેમ તે તૈયાર કરેલું હતું. રાજ્યાસનમાંથી મોટી વાણી એમ કહેતી મેં સાંભળી કે, ‘જુઓ, ઈશ્વરનું રહેઠાણ માણસોની સાથે છે, અને ઈશ્વર તેઓની સાથે વસશે, અને તેઓ તેમના લોકો થશે, અને ઈશ્વર પોતે તેઓની સાથે રહીને તેઓના ઈશ્વર થશે.	પ્રકટીકરણ ૨૧:૨-૩	ઇબ્રાહિમ જે જગ્યા વારસામાં પામવાનો હતો, તેમાં જવાને તેડું પામીને આજ્ઞાધીન થયો, એટલે પોતે ક્યાં જાય છે, એ ન જાણ્યાં છતાં વિશ્વાસથી તે રવાના થયો.	હિબ્રૂઓને मनुष्यों के बीच में परमेश्वर का निवास! अब परमेश्वर उनके बीच निवास करेंगे. वे उनकी प्रजा होंगे तथा स्वयं परमेश्वर उनके बीच होंगे.	प्रकाशित वाक्य 21:2-3	यह विश्वास ही था, जिसके द्वारा अब्राहाम ने परमेश्वर के बुलाने पर घर-परिवार का त्याग कर एक अन्य देश को चले जाने के लिए उनकी आज्ञा का पालन किया—वह देश, जो परमेश्वर उन्हें मीरास में देने पर थे.</Value><Br /><Value>वह यह जाने बिना ही चल पड़े कि वह कहां जा रहे थे.	इब्रानियों 11:8	जब फ़रोह ने प्रजा को वहां से जाने को कहा, तब परमेश्वर उन्हें फिलिस्तीनियों के देश में से होकर नहीं ले गए, यह रास्ता बहुत छोटा था. लेकिन परमेश्वर का कहना था, “लड़ाई देखकर लोग मिस्र देश वापस चले न जाएं.”	निर्गमन 13:17	क्योंकि मनुष्य का पुत्र यहां इसलिये नहीं आया कि अपनी सेवा करवाए, परंतु इसलिये कि सेवा करे और अनेकों की छुड़ौती के लिए अपना जीवन बलिदान कर दे.	मरकुस 10:45	यह पत्र पौलॉस की ओर से है, जो मसीह येशु का दास है, जिसका आगमन एक प्रेरित के रूप में हुआ तथा जो परमेश्वर के उस ईश्वरीय सुसमाचार के लिए अलग किया गया है,	रोमियों 1:1	इसलिये यहां से जाते हुए तुम सारे राष्ट्रों को मेरा शिष्य बनाओ और उन्हें पिता, पुत्र और पवित्र आत्मा के नाम में बपतिस्मा दो.	मत्ती 28:19	END

तो भी निकल गया।	इब्रानियों ११:८	जब फ़िरौन ने लोगों को जाने की आज्ञा दे दी, तब यद्यपि पलिश्तियों के देश में होकर जो मार्ग जाता है वह छोटा था;</Value><Br /><Value>तो भी परमेश्वर यह सोचकर उनको उस मार्ग से नहीं ले गया कि कहीं ऐसा न हो कि जब ये लोग लड़ाई देखें तब पछताकर मिस्र को लौट आएँ।	निर्गमन १३:१७	क्योंकि मनुष्य का पुत्र इसलिए नहीं आया, कि उसकी सेवा टहल की जाए, पर इसलिए आया, कि आप सेवा टहल करे, और बहुतों के छुटकारे के लिये अपना प्राण दे।	मरकुस १०:४५	पौलुस की ओर से जो यीशु मसीह का दास है, और प्रेरित होने के लिये बुलाया गया, और परमेश्वर के उस सुसमाचार के लिये अलग किया गया है	रोमियों १:१	इसलिए तुम जाकर सब जातियों के लोगों को चेला बनाओ; അവിടന്ന് അവരുടെ ഇടയിൽ വസിക്കും. അവർ അവിടത്തെ സ്വന്തം ജനമായിരിക്കും. ദൈവംതന്നെ അവരോടുകൂടെയിരുന്ന് അവരുടെ സ്വന്തം ദൈവമായിരിക്കുകയും ചെയ്യും.	വെളിപാട് 21:2-3	അബ്രാഹാം തനിക്ക് ഓഹരിയായി ലഭിക്കാനിരുന്ന ദേശത്തേക്കു പോകാൻ വിളിക്കപ്പെട്ടപ്പോൾ താൻ എവിടേക്കു പോകുന്നു</Value><Br /><Value>എന്നറിയാതെ വിശ്വാസത്താൽ അനുസരണയോടെ യാത്രപുറപ്പെട്ടു.	എബ്രായർ 11:8	ഫറവോൻ ജനത്തെ വിട്ടയച്ചപ്പോൾ, ഫെലിസ്ത്യദേശത്തുകൂടിയുള്ള വഴി ദൂരം കുറഞ്ഞതായിരുന്നെങ്കിലും ദൈവം അവരെ ആ വഴിയിൽക്കൂടി നടത്തിയില്ല. “യുദ്ധം നേരിട്ടാൽ അവർക്കു മനംമാറ്റം ഉണ്ടാകുകയും അവർ ഈജിപ്റ്റിലേക്കു മടങ്ങുകയും ചെയ്തേക്കാം,” എന്നു ദൈവം കരുതി.	പുറപ്പാട് 13:17	മനുഷ്യപുത്രൻ (ഞാൻ) വന്നതോ മറ്റുള്ളവരിൽനിന്ന് ശുശ്രൂഷ സ്വീകരിക്കാനല്ല; മറിച്ച്, മറ്റുള്ളവരെ ശുശ്രൂഷിക്കാനും തന്റെ ജീവൻ അനേകർക്ക് വീണ്ടെടുപ്പുവിലയായി നൽകാനും ആണ്.	മർക്കൊസ് 10:45	ക്രിസ്തുയേശുവിന്റെ ദാസനും അപ്പൊസ്തലനും ദൈവത്തിന്റെ സുവിശേഷം പ്രസംഗിക്കുന്നതിനു</Value><Br /><Value>നിയോഗിക്കപ്പെട്ടിരിക്കുന്നവനുമായ പൗലോസാണ് ഈ ലേഖനം എഴുതുന്നത്.	റോമർ 1:1	അതുകൊണ്ട് നിങ്ങൾ പോയി പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും നാമത്തിൽ സ്നാനം കഴിപ്പിച്ചും ഞാൻ നിങ്ങളോട് കൽപ്പിച്ചതെല്ലാം അനുവർത്തിക്കാൻ അവരെ ഉപദേശിച്ചുംകൊണ്ട് സകലജനതയെയും എന്റെ ശിഷ്യരാക്കുക.	മത്തായി 28:19	END

Yohani 3:16			Yesu kalonga, “Tati guwalekeziyi toziya wavimana ndiri vyawatenda.”</Value><Br /><Value>Shakapanu wagawana nguwu zyakuwi kwa kugalambula simbi.	Luka 23:34	Nuluwona lushi lunanagala, Yerusalemu ya syayi, palusuluka kulawa kumpindi kwa Mlungu. Luweriti litandirwa weri gambira mdala gwa ndowa yakaheripizitwi kala kuliwona na mpalu gwakuwi. Shakapanu mpikaniriti liziwu likulu kulawa mushibanta sha ufalumi lilonga, “Guloli! Kaya ya Mlungu pamuhera na wantu. ပိတရေတာန် က္ၐမသွ ယတ ဧတေ ယတ် ကရ္မ္မ ကုရွွန္တိ တန် န ဝိဒုး;</Value><Br /><Value>ပၑ္စာတ္တေ ဂုဋိကာပါတံ ကၖတွာ တသျ ဝသ္တြာဏိ ဝိဘဇျ ဇဂၖဟုး၊	လူကး 23:34	အပရံ သွရ္ဂာဒ် အဝရောဟန္တီ ပဝိတြာ နဂရီ, အရ္ထတော နဝီနာ ယိရူၑာလမပုရီ မယာ ဒၖၐ္ဋာ, သာ ဝရာယ ဝိဘူၐိတာ ကနျေဝ သုသဇ္ဇိတာသီတ်၊ အနန္တရံ သွရ္ဂာဒ် ဧၐ မဟာရဝေါ မယာ ၑြုတး ပၑျာယံ မာနဝဲး သာရ္ဒ္ဓမ် ဤၑွရသျာဝါသး, သ တဲး သာရ္ဒ္ဓံ ဝတ္သျတိ တေ</Value><Br /><Value>စ တသျ ပြဇာ ဘဝိၐျန္တိ, ဤၑွရၑ္စ သွယံ တေၐာမ် ဤၑွရော ဘူတွာ တဲး သာရ္ဒ္ဓံ သ္ထာသျတိ၊	ပြကာၑိတံ 21:2-3	ဝိၑွာသေနေဗြာဟီမ် အာဟူတး သန် အာဇ္ဉာံ ဂၖဟီတွာ ယသျ သ္ထာနသျာဓိကာရသ္တေန ပြာပ္တဝျသ္တတ် သ္ထာနံ ပြသ္ထိတဝါန် ကိန္တု ပြသ္ထာနသမယေ က္က ယာမီတိ နာဇာနာတ်၊	ဣဗြိဏး 11:8	အီ​ဂျစ်​ဘု​ရင်​သည်​ဣသ​ရေ​လ​အ​မျိုး​သား တို့​အား​ထွက်​ခွင့်​ပြု​သော​အ​ခါ ထာ​ဝ​ရ ဘု​ရား​သည်​ဖိ​လိတ္တိ​မြို့​သို့​သွား​သော​ပင် လယ်​ကမ်း​ခြေ​ဖြတ်​လမ်း​ဖြင့် သူ​တို့​ကို​ပို့ ဆောင်​တော်​မ​မူ။ သူ​တို့​သည်​စစ်​ပွဲ​တိုက်​ရ​မည် ကို​သိ​မြင်​လျှင်​စိတ်​ပြောင်း​၍ အီ​ဂျစ်​ပြည် သို့​ပြန်​သွား​ကြ​မည်​ဖြစ်​ကြောင်း​ဘု​ရား​သ​ခင်​သိ​တော်​မူ​၏။	ထွက်မြောက်ရာ ၁၃:၁၇	ယတော မနုၐျပုတြး သေဝျော ဘဝိတုံ နာဂတး သေဝါံ ကရ္တ္တာံ တထာနေကေၐာံ ပရိတြာဏသျ မူလျရူပသွပြာဏံ ဒါတုဉ္စာဂတး၊	မာရ္ကး 10:45	ဤၑွရော နိဇပုတြမဓိ ယံ သုသံဝါဒံ ဘဝိၐျဒွါဒိဘိ ရ္ဓရ္မ္မဂြန္ထေ ပြတိၑြုတဝါန် တံ သုသံဝါဒံ ပြစာရယိတုံ ပၖထက္ကၖတ အာဟူတး ပြေရိတၑ္စ ပြဘော ရျီၑုခြီၐ္ဋသျ သေဝကော ယး ပေါ်လး	ရောမိဏး 1:1	အတော ယူယံ ပြယာယ သရွွဒေၑီယာန် ၑိၐျာန် ကၖတွာ ပိတုး ပုတြသျ ပဝိတြသျာတ္မနၑ္စ နာမ္နာ တာနဝဂါဟယတ; အဟံ ယုၐ္မာန် ယဒျဒါဒိၑံ 21:2-3	વિશ્વાસેનેબ્રાહીમ્ આહૂતઃ સન્ આજ્ઞાં ગૃહીત્વા યસ્ય સ્થાનસ્યાધિકારસ્તેન પ્રાપ્તવ્યસ્તત્ સ્થાનં પ્રસ્થિતવાન્ કિન્તુ પ્રસ્થાનસમયે ક્ક યામીતિ નાજાનાત્	ઇબ્રિણઃ 11:8	જ્યારે ફારુને લોકોને જવા દીઘા ત્યારે એમ બન્યું કે પલિસ્તીઓના દેશમાં થઈને જવાનો રસ્તો ટૂંકો હોવા છતાં પણ તે રસ્તે તેઓને લઈ ગયા નહિ.</Value><Br /><Value>કેમ કે યહોવાહે વિચાર્યું કે, “રખેને યુદ્ધ થાય અને લોકો પોતાનો વિચાર બદલી પાછા મિસર ચાલ્યા જાય.”	નિર્ગમન ૧૩:૧૭	યતો મનુષ્યપુત્રઃ સેવ્યો ભવિતું નાગતઃ સેવાં કર્ત્તાં તથાનેકેષાં પરિત્રાણસ્ય મૂલ્યરૂપસ્વપ્રાણં દાતુઞ્ચાગતઃ	માર્કઃ 10:45	ઈશ્વરો નિજપુત્રમધિ યં સુસંવાદં ભવિષ્યદ્વાદિભિ ર્ધર્મ્મગ્રન્થે પ્રતિશ્રુતવાન્ તં સુસંવાદં પ્રચારયિતું પૃથક્કૃત આહૂતઃ પ્રેરિતશ્ચ પ્રભો ર્યીશુખ્રીષ્ટસ્ય સેવકો યઃ પૌલઃ	રોમિણઃ 1:1	અતો યૂયં પ્રયાય સર્વ્વદેશીયાન્ શિષ્યાન્ કૃત્વા પિતુઃ પુત્રસ્ય પવિત્રસ્યાત્મનશ્ચ નામ્ના તાનવગાહયત; અહં યુષ્માન્ યદ્યદાદિશં તદપિ પાલયિતું તાનુપાદિશત	મથિઃ 28:19	END

ಮಾನವೈಃ ಸಾರ್ದ್ಧಮ್ ಈಶ್ವರಸ್ಯಾವಾಸಃ, ಸ ತೈಃ ಸಾರ್ದ್ಧಂ ವತ್ಸ್ಯತಿ ತೇ ಚ ತಸ್ಯ ಪ್ರಜಾ ಭವಿಷ್ಯನ್ತಿ,</Value><Br /><Value>ಈಶ್ವರಶ್ಚ ಸ್ವಯಂ ತೇಷಾಮ್ ಈಶ್ವರೋ ಭೂತ್ವಾ ತೈಃ ಸಾರ್ದ್ಧಂ ಸ್ಥಾಸ್ಯತಿ	ಪ್ರಕಾಶಿತಂ 21:2-3	ವಿಶ್ವಾಸೇನೇಬ್ರಾಹೀಮ್ ಸಮೀಪವಿದ್ದರೂ ದೇವರು ಅವರನ್ನು ಅದರಲ್ಲಿ ನಡೆಸಲಿಲ್ಲ.</Value><Br /><Value>ಏಕೆಂದರೆ ದೇವರು, “ಜನರು ಯುದ್ಧವನ್ನು ನೋಡಿ, ಮನಸ್ಸನ್ನು ಬೇರೆಮಾಡಿಕೊಂಡು, ಈಜಿಪ್ಟಿಗೆ ಹಿಂದಿರುಗಿಯಾರು,” ಎಂದು ಹೇಳಿದರು.	ವಿಮೋಚನಕಾಂಡ 13:17	ಯತೋ ಮನುಷ್ಯಪುತ್ರಃ ಸೇವ್ಯೋ ಭವಿತುಂ ನಾಗತಃ ಸೇವಾಂ ಕರ್ತ್ತಾಂ ತಥಾನೇಕೇಷಾಂ ಪರಿತ್ರಾಣಸ್ಯ ಮೂಲ್ಯರೂಪಸ್ವಪ್ರಾಣಂ ದಾತುಞ್ಚಾಗತಃ	ಮಾರ್ಕಃ 10:45	ಈಶ್ವರೋ ನಿಜಪುತ್ರಮಧಿ ಯಂ ಸುಸಂವಾದಂ ಭವಿಷ್ಯದ್ವಾದಿಭಿ ರ್ಧರ್ಮ್ಮಗ್ರನ್ಥೇ ಪ್ರತಿಶ್ರುತವಾನ್ ತಂ പശ്ചാത്തേ ഗുടികാപാതം കൃത്വാ തസ്യ വസ്ത്രാണി വിഭജ്യ ജഗൃഹുഃ	ലൂകഃ 23:34	അപരം സ്വർഗാദ് അവരോഹന്തീ പവിത്രാ നഗരീ, അർഥതോ നവീനാ യിരൂശാലമപുരീ മയാ ദൃഷ്ടാ, സാ വരായ വിഭൂഷിതാ കന്യേവ സുസജ്ജിതാസീത് അനന്തരം സ്വർഗാദ് ഏഷ മഹാരവോ മയാ ശ്രുതഃ പശ്യായം മാനവൈഃ സാർദ്ധമ് ഈശ്വരസ്യാവാസഃ, സ തൈഃ സാർദ്ധം വത്സ്യതി തേ ച തസ്യ പ്രജാ ഭവിഷ്യന്തി, ഈശ്വരശ്ച സ്വയം തേഷാമ് ഈശ്വരോ ഭൂത്വാ തൈഃ സാർദ്ധം സ്ഥാസ്യതി	പ്രകാശിതം 21:2-3	വിശ്വാസേനേബ്രാഹീമ് ആഹൂതഃ സൻ ആജ്ഞാം ഗൃഹീത്വാ യസ്യ സ്ഥാനസ്യാധികാരസ്തേന പ്രാപ്തവ്യസ്തത്</Value><Br /><Value>സ്ഥാനം പ്രസ്ഥിതവാൻ കിന്തു പ്രസ്ഥാനസമയേ ക്ക യാമീതി നാജാനാത്	ഇബ്രിണഃ 11:8	ഫറവോൻ ജനത്തെ വിട്ടയച്ച ശേഷം ഫെലിസ്ത്യരുടെ ദേശത്ത് കൂടിയുള്ള വഴി എളുപ്പമായിരുന്നു. എങ്കിലും ജനം യുദ്ധം കാണുമ്പോൾ അനുതപിച്ച് ഈജിപ്റ്റിലേയ്ക്ക് മടങ്ങിപ്പോകുമെന്ന് വിചാരിച്ച് ദൈവം അവരെ അതിലെ കൊണ്ടുപോയില്ല;	പുറപ്പാട് ൧൩:൧൭	യതോ മനുഷ്യപുത്രഃ സേവ്യോ ഭവിതും നാഗതഃ സേവാം കർത്താം തഥാനേകേഷാം പരിത്രാണസ്യ മൂല്യരൂപസ്വപ്രാണം ദാതുഞ്ചാഗതഃ	മാർകഃ 10:45	ഈശ്വരോ നിജപുത്രമധി യം സുസംവാദം ഭവിഷ്യദ്വാദിഭി ർധർമ്മഗ്രന്ഥേ പ്രതിശ്രുതവാൻ തം സുസംവാദം പ്രചാരയിതും പൃഥക്കൃത ആഹൂതഃ പ്രേരിതശ്ച പ്രഭോ ര്യീശുഖ്രീഷ്ടസ്യ സേവകോ യഃ പൗലഃ	രോമിണഃ 1:1	അതോ യൂയം പ്രയായ സർവ്വദേശീയാൻ ശിഷ്യാൻ കൃത്വാ പിതുഃ പുത്രസ്യ പവിത്രസ്യാത്മനശ്ച നാമ്നാ താനവഗാഹയത;</Value><Br /><Value>അഹം യുഷ്മാൻ യദ്യദാദിശം തദപി പാലയിതും താനുപാദിശത	മഥിഃ 28:19	END

విభూషితా కన్యేవ సుసజ్జితాసీత్ అనన్తరం స్వర్గాద్ ఏష మహారవో మయా శ్రుతః పశ్యాయం మానవైః సార్ద్ధమ్ ఈశ్వరస్యావాసః, స తైః సార్ద్ధం వత్స్యతి తే చ తస్య ప్రజా భవిష్యన్తి, ఈశ్వరశ్చ స్వయం తేషామ్ ఈశ్వరో భూత్వా తైః సార్ద్ధం స్థాస్యతి	ప్రకాశితం 21:2-3	విశ్వాసేనేబ్రాహీమ్ ఆహూతః సన్ ఆజ్ఞాం గృహీత్వా యస్య స్థానస్యాధికారస్తేన ప్రాప్తవ్యస్తత్ స్థానం ప్రస్థితవాన్ కిన్తు ప్రస్థానసమయే క్క యామీతి నాజానాత్	ఇబ్రిణః 11:8	ఫరో ఆ ప్రజలను వెళ్ళనిచ్చినప్పుడు దేవుడు వాళ్ళను ఫిలిష్తీయ దేశం నుండి దగ్గర దారి అయినప్పటికీ ఆ దారిన వాళ్ళను వెళ్లనీయలేదు.</Value><Br /><Value>“ఈ ప్రజలు ఫిలిష్తీయులతో జరిగే యుద్ధం చూసి మనసు మార్చుకుని తిరిగి ఐగుప్తుకు వెళ్లిపోతారేమో” అనుకున్నాడు.	నిర్గమకాండము ౧౩:౧౭	యతో మనుష్యపుత్రః సేవ్యో భవితుం నాగతః సేవాం కర్త్తాం తథానేకేషాం పరిత్రాణస్య మూల్యరూపస్వప్రాణం దాతుఞ్చాగతః	మార్కః 10:45	ఈశ్వరో నిజపుత్రమధి యం సుసంవాదం భవిష్యద్వాదిభి ర్ధర్మ్మగ్రన్థే ప్రతిశ్రుతవాన్ తం సుసంవాదం ప్రచారయితుం పృథక్కృత ఆహూతః ప్రేరితశ్చ ప్రభో ర్యీశుఖ్రీష్టస్య సేవకో యః పౌలః	రోమిణః 1:1	అతో యూయం ప్రయాయ సర్వ్వదేశీయాన్ శిష్యాన్ కృత్వా పితుః పుత్రస్య పవిత్రస్యాత్మనశ్చ నామ్నా తానవగాహయత; అహం యుష్మాన్ యద్యదాదిశం తదపి పాలయితుం తానుపాదిశత	మథిః 28:19	END

Narinig ko ang isang malakas na tinig mula sa trono sinasabing: “Tingnan mo! Ang tirahan ng Diyos ay kasama ng mga tao, at siya ay naninirahan kasama nila. Sila ay magiging kaniyang bayan, at ang Diyos mismo ay makakasama nila at siya ay magiging kanilang Diyos.”	Pahayag 21:2-3	Sa pamamagitan ito ng pananampalataya na si Abraham nang siya ay tinawag, Siya ay sumunod at nagtungo sa lugar na kaniyang tatanggapin bilang isang tagapagmana. Pumunta siya na hindi niya nalalaman kung saan siya tutungo.	Mga Hebreo 11:8	Nang pinayagan ni Paraon na umalis ang mga tao, hindi sila pinangunahan ng Diyos sa landas patungo sa lupain ng mga Palestina, kahit pa malapit ang lupain. Marcos 10:45	Ako si Pablo, na isang lingkod ni Jesu-Cristo, tinawag upang maging apostol, at inilaan para sa ebanghelyo ng Diyos.	Mga Roma 1:1	Humayo kayo at gawing mga alagad ang lahat ng mga bansa. அது தனது கணவனுக்காக அழகாய் அலங்கரிக்கப்பட்ட, ஒரு மணமகளைப்போல் ஆயத்தமாக்கப்பட்டிருந்தது. அப்பொழுது நான், அரியணையில் இருந்து வருகின்ற, ஒரு பெரும் குரல் இவ்வாறு சொல்வதைக் கேட்டேன்: “இறைவன் தங்குகின்ற இடம், இப்பொழுது மனிதருடன் இருக்கின்றது. அவர் மனிதருடனேயே குடியிருப்பார். அவர்கள் அவருடைய மக்களாயிருப்பார்கள். இறைவன் தாமே அவர்களுடன் இருந்து, அவர்களுடைய இறைவனாயிருப்பார்.	வெளிப்படுத்தின விசேஷம் 21:2-3	விசுவாசத்தினாலேயே ஆபிரகாம் தான் உரிமைச்சொத்தாகப் பெறவிருந்த இடத்திற்குப் போகும்படி அழைக்கப்பட்டபோது,</Value><Br /><Value>தான் எங்கே போகிறேன் என்றுகூட அவன் அறியாதிருந்ததும் கீழ்ப்படிந்து புறப்பட்டான்.	எபிரேயர் 11:8	பார்வோன் இஸ்ரயேலரைப் போகவிட்டபின்பு, பெலிஸ்தியரின் நாட்டின் வழி குறுகியதாக இருந்தபோதிலும், இறைவன் அவர்களை அதன் வழியாக நடத்திச் செல்லவில்லை. ஏனெனில், “அவர்கள் யுத்தத்தை எதிர்கொண்டால், தங்கள் மனதை மாற்றி எகிப்திற்குத் திரும்பிவிடுவார்கள்” என இறைவன் சொன்னார்.	யாத்திராகமம் 13:17	மானிடமகனாகிய நானும் பணிவிடையைப் பெற்றுக்கொள்ள அல்ல, பணிவிடை செய்யவே வந்தேன்;</Value><Br /><Value>அநேகரை மீட்கும்படி என் உயிரைக் கொடுக்கவும் வந்தேன்” என்றார்.	மாற்கு 10:45	கிறிஸ்து இயேசுவின் ஊழியனாய் இருக்கின்ற பவுலாகிய நான் அப்போஸ்தலனாய் இருக்கும்படி அழைக்கப்பட்டிருக்கிறேன்.</Value><Br /><Value>இறைவனுடைய நற்செய்தியை அறிவிப்பதற்காகப் பிரித்தெடுக்கப்பட்டும் இருக்கிறேன்.	ரோமர் 1:1	எனவே நீங்கள் புறப்பட்டுப்போய் எல்லா நாட்டின் மக்களையும் எனக்குச் சீடராக்குங்கள். பிதா, மகன்,</Value><Br /><Value>பரிசுத்த ஆவியானவருடைய பெயரில் அவர்களுக்கு திருமுழுக்கு கொடுத்து,	மத்தேயு 28:19	END
